 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">2.02</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Results of Operations and Financial Condition</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;13, 2022, Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ended August&#160;31, 2022 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">Fourth Quarter Results Ahead of Expectations; Raising Long-Term Targets for U.S. Healthcare Segment </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fourth quarter and fiscal year financial highlights </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Fourth quarter loss per share* from continuing operations was $0.48, a decrease of $0.89 from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; adjusted earnings per share (EPS*) decreased 31.8&nbsp;percent to $0.80, down 30.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting a strong prior year quarter with higher <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccination volumes </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Fiscal 2022 EPS from continuing operations was $5.01, an increase of 117.6&nbsp;percent, compared with $2.30 in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period; adjusted EPS increased 2.5&nbsp;percent to $5.04, up 3.4&nbsp;percent in constant currency </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Fourth quarter sales from continuing operations decreased 5.3&nbsp;percent year-over-year, to $32.4&nbsp;billion, down
3.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, including a 660 basis point impact from the anticipated sales decline at AllianceRx Walgreens </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Fiscal 2022 sales from continuing operations increased 0.1&nbsp;percent to $132.7&nbsp;billion, up 1.2&nbsp;percent on a
constant currency basis, including a 550 basis point impact from AllianceRx Walgreens </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fiscal 2023 guidance and long-term growth outlook
</I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B><I></I></B>Expecting fiscal year 2023 adjusted EPS of $4.45 to $4.65 as strong core business growth is more than offset
by lapping fiscal year 2022 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> execution, and currency headwinds </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Raising U.S. Healthcare fiscal 2025 sales target to $11&nbsp;billion to $12&nbsp;billion, with the segment expected to
achieve positive adjusted EBITDA by fiscal year 2024 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Increased visibility to the company&#146;s long-term growth algorithm, building to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-teens</FONT> adjusted EPS growth in fiscal year 2025 and beyond </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill., Oct.
13,&nbsp;2022&#151;Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the fiscal year and fourth quarter that ended Aug. 31, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Chief Executive Officer Rosalind Brewer said: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;WBA has
delivered ahead of expectations in the first year of our transformation to a consumer-centric healthcare company. Our resilient business achieved growth while navigating macroeconomic headwinds. Fiscal 2023 will be a year of accelerating core growth
and rapidly scaling our U.S. Healthcare business. Our execution to date provides us visibility and confidence to increase the long-term outlook for our next growth engine and reconfirm our path to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-teens</FONT>
adjusted EPS growth. Our strategic actions are unlocking sustainable shareholder value as we simplify the company and continue our journey to being a healthcare leader.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fourth Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA fourth quarter
sales from continuing operations decreased 5.3&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $32.4&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 3.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Sales growth at Walgreens and in the
International segment, and sales contributions from the U.S. Healthcare segment were more than offset by a 660 basis point impact from the sales decline at AllianceRx Walgreens. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">1 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fourth quarter operating loss from continuing operations was $822&nbsp;million compared to operating income
of $910&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating loss in the quarter reflects a $783&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charge related to intangible assets in Boots
UK, and higher costs related to the Transformational Cost Management Program. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations was $744&nbsp;million, a decrease of 38.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower U.S. pharmacy
operating results as it lapped higher volumes of prior year <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations, and growth investments in U.S. Healthcare, partly offset by improved retail contributions in both the U.S. Retail Pharmacy and
International segments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss from continuing operations in the fourth quarter was $415&nbsp;million compared to net income of $358&nbsp;million in
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting the decline in operating income, which was partly offset by the favorable impact of a lower tax rate, and a gain on the sale of a portion of the Company&#146;s equity method
investment in Option Care Health. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations decreased 31.9&nbsp;percent to $694&nbsp;million, down 30.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Loss per share from continuing operations was $0.48, compared to earnings per share of $0.41 in
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted earnings per share from continuing operations decreased 31.8&nbsp;percent to $0.80, reflecting a decrease of 30.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $85&nbsp;million in the fourth quarter and free cash flow was $(407) million, a $1.3&nbsp;billion decrease compared with
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter driven primarily by lower operating income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-buy</FONT> of seasonal inventory, U.S. legal settlements, and increased capital expenditures in growth
initiatives, partly offset by working capital timing benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal Year Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales from continuing operations in fiscal 2022 increased 0.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to
$132.7&nbsp;billion, up 1.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis,<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP>reflecting comparable sales growth at Walgreens and in the International segment as well as contributions from U.S.
Healthcare acquisitions, partly offset by a 550 basis point impact from the sales decline at AllianceRx Walgreens. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income from continuing
operations in fiscal 2022 decreased 40.8&nbsp;percent to $1.4&nbsp;billion, compared with $2.3&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. This reflects a $783&nbsp;million Boots UK impairment charge, a
$683&nbsp;million charge related to the opioid settlement with the State of Florida, and higher Transformational Cost Management program costs, partly offset by a $1.5&nbsp;billion charge in the prior fiscal year related to the Company&#146;s equity
earnings from AmerisourceBergen. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations increased 0.3&nbsp;percent on a reported basis to $5.1&nbsp;billion, up 1.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increase reflects improved retail
contribution in the U.S., and a continued rebound in International sales and profitability, partly offset by a decrease in U.S. pharmacy operating results, and by growth investments in U.S. Healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings from continuing operations were $4.3&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2022, compared with $2.0&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
period, reflecting a $2.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain in the first quarter due to the remeasurement of the Company&#146;s previously held investments in VillageMD and Shields Health Solutions, and a
$1.2&nbsp;billion charge, net of tax, in the prior fiscal year from the Company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. This was partly offset by impairment charges in Boots UK in the fourth quarter, and the charge related to the Florida opioid
settlement in the third quarter. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations increased 2.5&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to $4.4&nbsp;billion, up 3.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency
basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS from continuing operations for fiscal 2022 increased to $5.01, compared with $2.30 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period.
Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $5.04, an increase of 2.5&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and an increase of 3.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">2 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $3.9&nbsp;billion in fiscal 2022. Free cash flow was $2.2&nbsp;billion,
a decrease of $2.0&nbsp;billion from fiscal 2021 driven by lower free cash flow from the AllianceRx Walgreens business, the absence of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related government support, seasonal inventory <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-buy,</FONT> U.S. legal settlements, and increased capital expenditures in growth initiatives, including the VillageMD footprint expansion, the rollout of microfulfillment centers, and digital transformation
initiatives, partly offset by working capital initiatives and timing benefits. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA continued to achieve strong results across its business, including: </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company has changed the names of two reportable
segments to better align with the Company&#146;s business activities, structure, and strategy. The &#147;United States&#148; segment has been renamed to &#147;U.S. Retail Pharmacy&#148; and the &#147;Walgreens Health&#148; segment was renamed to
&#147;U.S. Healthcare&#148;. The segment name changes did not result in any change to the composition of the segments. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">3 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>U.S. Retail Pharmacy </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had fourth quarter sales of $26.7&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 7.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 1.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter and lapped strong comparable sales of 8.1&nbsp;percent in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, which included a significant contribution from
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales decreased 8.8&nbsp;percent compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, negatively impacted by a 10 percentage point headwind from AllianceRx Walgreens. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 3.0&nbsp;percent in the fourth quarter compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable prescriptions filled in the fourth quarter decreased 3.5&nbsp;percent while comparable prescriptions excluding immunizations decreased 0.1&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents, decreased 4.4&nbsp;percent to 298.7&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales decreased 2.4&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales decreased 1.9&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. Excluding tobacco, comparable retail sales decreased 1.1&nbsp;percent. Comparable retail sales lapped strong results in the year ago quarter where comparable retail sales increased 6.2&nbsp;percent, aided by broad based growth across all
categories including strong sales of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related items. Over a three-year period, comparable retail sales excluding tobacco increased 13.0&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 15.3&nbsp;percent to $5.3&nbsp;billion compared to $6.3&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted
gross profit decreased 13.2&nbsp;percent to $5.4&nbsp;billion compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting a decline in pharmacy results from lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations
and continued reimbursement pressure, partly offset by retail gross margin performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) decreased
3.2&nbsp;percent to $5.2&nbsp;billion compared to $5.3&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 6.8&nbsp;percent to $4.8&nbsp;billion, driven by lower volumes of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and cost discipline, partly offset by increased labor costs and the timing of marketing expenditures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the fourth quarter decreased 75.2&nbsp;percent to $251&nbsp;million compared to operating income of $1.0&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting higher costs related to the Transformational Cost Management Program. Adjusted operating income decreased 36.1&nbsp;percent to $786&nbsp;million compared to $1.2&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccination volumes and continued reimbursement pressure, partly offset by improved retail gross margin and SG&amp;A expense
improvement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The International segment had fourth quarter
sales of $5.1&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 6.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 13.3&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 6.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis,
with Boots UK sales growing 6.0&nbsp;percent, and the Company&#146;s German wholesale business growing 6.8&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales
decreased 6.9&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, largely due to lower demand for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> services compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 15.2&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, with notable market share gains in Personal Care and
Health and Wellness. Footfall improved around 20&nbsp;percent, compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots.com continued to perform well, accounting for 11&nbsp;percent of retail sales in the quarter compared to
6&nbsp;percent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 7.3&nbsp;percent compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 12.7&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross profit increased 5.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong sales growth across all
International markets, partially offset by lower demand for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related services in the UK compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter and timing of National Health Service
(NHS) reimbursement. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">4 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in the quarter increased 54.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter
to $1.8&nbsp;billion, due to impairment charges in Boots UK. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased 1.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting increased in store activity and absence of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related
government support compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss in the fourth quarter was $672&nbsp;million compared
to operating income of $46&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, as a result of the $783&nbsp;million impairment charges in Boots UK. Adjusted operating income grew to $163&nbsp;million, an increase of
31.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>U.S. Healthcare </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
U.S. Healthcare segment had fourth quarter sales of $622&nbsp;million. On a pro forma basis, this segment&#146;s businesses grew sales at a combined rate of 34&nbsp;percent in the quarter. Shields grew 48&nbsp;percent, driven by key contract wins,
further expansion of existing partnerships, and strong executional focus. VillageMD grew 31&nbsp;percent, reflecting existing clinic growth and clinic footprint expansion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit was a loss of $37&nbsp;million and adjusted gross profit was a loss of $9&nbsp;million. Shields gross profit, driven by further growth of existing
partnerships and expanding margins, was more than offset by VillageMD expansion. As of the end of the fourth quarter, VillageMD had 334 total clinics open, an increase of 82 clinics compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Fourth quarter SG&amp;A was $301&nbsp;million, and adjusted SG&amp;A was $143&nbsp;million, reflecting the two acquisitions, as well as continued
investments in the Walgreens Health organic business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss was $338&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating loss was $151&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating loss
excludes certain costs related to stock compensation expense and amortization of acquired intangible assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Fiscal 2023 Outlook and Long-Term Growth Outlook
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the full fiscal year 2023, Walgreens Boots Alliance expects adjusted EPS of $4.45 to $4.65. Healthy core business growth of 8 to 10&nbsp;percent in constant
currency is expected to be more than offset by adverse currency movements of approximately 2&nbsp;percent and by a headwind of 15 to 17&nbsp;percent from lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccination volumes. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Additionally, the Company is raising the U.S. Healthcare fiscal year 2025 sales target to $11&nbsp;billion to $12&nbsp;billion, from $9&nbsp;billion to $10&nbsp;billion
previously. The segment is expected to achieve positive adjusted EBITDA by fiscal year 2024. The Company reconfirmed its expectation to achieve <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-teens</FONT> adjusted EPS growth in fiscal year 2025. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Management will provide additional details during the earnings call presentation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will hold an extended conference call to discuss fourth
quarter and fiscal 2022 earnings results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, Oct. 13, 2022. The conference call will be approximately two hours in length, including Q&amp;A, and simulcast through the WBA investor relations website at:
http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A replay of the conference call will be archived on the website for 12 months after the call. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">*All references to net
earnings or net loss are to net earnings or net loss attributable to WBA, and all references to EPS are to diluted EPS attributable to WBA. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">**&#147;Adjusted,&#148;
&#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP measure. The Company defines Adjusted EBITDA as segment operating income/(loss) before depreciation, amortization, and stock-based compensation; in addition to these items, the
Company excludes certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments, when they occur, as further defined. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">5 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Please refer to the supplemental information presented below for reconciliations of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures used in
this release to the most comparable GAAP financial measure and related disclosures. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>ENDS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 13,000 locations
across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the healthcare ecosystem. The Company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health.
Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare.
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">6 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA has more than 315,000 team members and a presence in nine countries through its portfolio of consumer brands:
Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty Company, Benavides in Mexico and Ahumada in Chile. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been recognized for
its commitment to operating sustainably: it is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI) and was named to the 100 Best Corporate Citizens 2021. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented
in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These
supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency
translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
Company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute
for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company does not provide
a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available
without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact
diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company also presents certain information related to
current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange
rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this
presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least
twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the past twelve months as well as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for the first
twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail
sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the Company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same
as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented
on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">11 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company considers certain metrics, such as comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions, and comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, number of payor/ provider partnerships, number of locations of Walgreens Health Corners, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-located</FONT> VillageMD clinics and number of
total VillageMD clinics, at period end, to be key performance indicators because the Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a
substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the total number of VillageMD clinics, clinics are defined as the primary care locations where the Company or the Company&#146;s affiliates lease or
license space and the providers are employed by either the Company or one of the Company&#146;s affiliates. These clinics are primarily branded as Village Medical where the Company employs the providers but, in some instances, may operate under
their own brands. </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen&#146;s recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its
financial statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and
contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated
by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an
intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to
measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments exclude the expected profit margin
component from cost of sales recorded under the business combination accounting principles. The stock based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting
and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these
arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings, including legal defense costs. In fiscal 2022, the Company recorded a $683&nbsp;million charge related to a settlement agreement with the State of Florida to resolve all claims related to the distribution and dispensing of prescription
opioid medications across the Company&#146;s pharmacies in the State of Florida. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges
enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include charges incurred related to certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in operating income, for example, costs related to integration efforts for merger, acquisition
and divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance and stock compensation. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing
and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of goodwill and intangible assets do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business. The
Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These
charges are recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">14 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for
using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices,
which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within Other income, net. We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying derivative
instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Impairment of equity method investment and investment in equity securities includes impairment of certain investments. The
Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because these do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s business and it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis. Exclusion of such charges enables more
consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Other income, net. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">In fiscal 2022, the Company finalized the working capital adjustments with AmerisourceBergen related to the sale of the
Alliance Healthcare business, resulting in a $38&nbsp;million charge recorded to Other income, net in the Consolidated Statement of Earnings. In fiscal 2021, the Company recorded a net gain of $322&nbsp;million within results of discontinued
operations related to the sale of the Alliance Healthcare business. This gain was excluded as it is not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">11</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on the sale of equity method investments. In fiscal 2022, the Company recorded a gain of
$417&nbsp;million and $145&nbsp;million in Other income, net due to a partial sale of its equity method investments in AmerisourceBergen and Option Care Health, respectively. In fiscal 2021, the Company recorded a gain of $290&nbsp;million in Other
income, net due to a partial sale of ownership interest in Option Care Health by the Company&#146;s then equity method investee HC Group Holdings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">12</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on business combinations due to the remeasurement of previously held minority equity interests
and debt securities to fair value. In fiscal 2022, the Company recorded such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gains of $2.2&nbsp;billion and $402&nbsp;million for VillageMD and Shields, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">In fiscal 2022, the Company incurred a $4&nbsp;million loss in connection with the early extinguishment of debt related to
the integration of Shields. In fiscal 2021, the Company incurred a $419&nbsp;million loss related to the Company&#146;s cash tender offers to partially purchase and retire $3.3&nbsp;billion of long-term U.S. denominated notes. The Company excludes
these charges as related activities do not reflect the Company&#146;s ongoing financial performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision (benefit) include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision (benefit) commensurate
with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. and U.K. tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income
tax provision (benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share of certain equity
method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded within post tax
earnings from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity method investments
are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that they do not reflect
all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. In fiscal 2021, due to partial sales of ownership interests in Option Care Health, our then equity method investee HC Group Holdings lost the ability to control Option Care Health and,
therefore, deconsolidated Option Care Health in its financial statements. As a result of this deconsolidation, HC Group Holdings recognized a gain of $1.2&nbsp;billion and the Company recorded its share of equity earnings in HC Group Holdings of
$576&nbsp;million. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from the reported net loss, the impact of potentially dilutive securities on the
per share amounts has been omitted from the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the three months ended August&nbsp;31, 2022. The impact of these potentially dilutive securities has been included in
the calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the twelve months ended August&nbsp;31, 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes impact of potentially dilutive securities in the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common shares, diluted
for adjusted diluted net earnings per common share calculation purposes for the three and twelve months ended August&nbsp;31, 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating income (loss) for U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment includes equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen. As a result
of the two month reporting lag, operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2022 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2022 through June&nbsp;30, 2022 and the period
of July&nbsp;1, 2021 through June&nbsp;30, 2022, respectively. Operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2021 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2021 through
June&nbsp;30, 2021, and the period of July&nbsp;1, 2020 through June&nbsp;30, 2021, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating margins and adjusted operating margins have been calculated excluding equity earnings (loss) in
AmerisourceBergen and adjusted equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating income (loss) for U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment includes equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen. As a result
of the two month reporting lag, operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2022 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2022 through June&nbsp;30, 2022 and the period
of July&nbsp;1, 2021 through June&nbsp;30, 2022, respectively. Operating income (loss) for the three and twelve month period ended August&nbsp;31, 2021 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings for the period of April&nbsp;1, 2021 through
June&nbsp;30, 2021, and the period of July&nbsp;1, 2020 through June&nbsp;30, 2021, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

AmerisourceBergen and adjusted equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

presentation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
